### Probability Mass Function

![Graph with seats probability mass function not yet produced](average-seats-pmf-familienparteideutschlandsepp.png "Seats Probability Mass Function")

The following table shows the probability mass function per seat for the [poll average](average.html) for Familienpartei Deutschlands (EPP).

| Number of Seats | Probability | Accumulated | Special Marks |
|:---------------:|:-----------:|:-----------:|:-------------:|
| 0 | 75% | 100% | Median |
| 1 | 25% | 25% | Last Result |
| 2 | 0% | 0% |  |
